< Review>
Would give it zero stars if it were possible. Based on service.

We came in to Dos Geckos at the recommendation of my coworker. We ordered around 2pm, the place was not busy. We sat and waited for 45 minutes while we watched everyone who had showed up after us get their food. I asked our server if she put our order in, she replied "yes I did". Well another server walked by again, dropping food to another table who had showed up long after we had, so I asked her if she could see if our order was put in, well she came back and told us the truth, which was that our server had NOT put our order in after all, and she offered us a free beer to make up for it. (That was nice, but it was now 2:45 and I had to be at work at 3:30 in Dunsmuir, that's why I got to the restaurant at 2pm.)
She told me I could eat it in my car while I drive to work. I told her I didn't come to this restaurant to eat and drive. I went back outside to our table, checked the time, noticed it was getting close to time I would need to leave and she comes outside and drops the bill at our table without a word. WE HAVE NOT EVEN GOTTEN ANY FOOD AT THIS TIME. That was the last straw.  My boyfriend went inside gave them the bill and we left. I asked for a manager before we left, they said there wasn't one there. If the owner reads this, I would really like to talk to you about our service on this day. I am a server/bartender In fine dining establishments and I am a very compassionate person. This experience was unacceptable by any measure.</Review>

I am a frequent customer to the Almaden Valley Nursery.  They high-quality plants and products.  The staff is very helpful.  In my experience, when one cannot answer a question, they find another staff person with the expertise.  In addition to plants, I now spend as much on the wonderful gift items available as you enter the store.  If you have shopped at the boutique at, for example, the Roberstville Carwash, then you need to try the AVN.  Jeni manages the gift shop.  There is a wonderful selection there of holiday decorations and handmade jewelry.  Additionally, if you are in to CA Native Plants (I am), you get a 10% discount if you show your CNPS membership card.  I special order native plants and they are delivered and sold at the same price of the nursery stock. I recommend the AV Nursery.<//review>

<userid>107444994278293202314< /userid>< Rating>
4</Rating>
<Review>Okay, it's a 99 Cents Only Store

And yet some items are $2.99, I saw one item for $4.99. Not like the good old days when absolutely everything in the store was 99 cents. Of course that's at all 99 Cents Only Stores, not just the one in Wilmington... And to be fair, some items are less than 99 cents. This is not one of your upscale 99 Cents Only Stores... (The ones with wine, at least 3 types of olive oil and a manager with a Pavillions attitude) But this one manages to cram a whole lot into a small space and the floor staff is forever straightening up the shelves and bins disrupted by the bargain hunters. There are to be sure, some strange products: Non Dairy Creamer that clearly states "Contains Milk" and Swedish Sardines from China. But to me, that's half the fun in going to the store in the first place: never knowing what I'm going to find. I have learned over the years that if I go to the 99 cent only store because I really truly need peanut butter then for certain, they will be out of peanut butter. On the other hand if I go in with a loosely drawn up list with no definitive needs, I'm likely to find almost everything I want. This store has a very Hands-On manager who is only too eager to help you and her staff has the same attitude. Even the security guards are pleasant which is a rare sight in Wilmington. So it's tiny store, the geraniums in front are sometimes wilted, the parking lot is crazed but it's still the best 99 Cent Only store in Wilmington. In fact, it's the only 99 Cents Only Store in Wilmington, despite many imitators.<//Review><pics>None</pics><response>{'time': 1494881428927, 'text': 'Hi John L. Kerr,  seeing 5 stars puts a smile on our face.  Hopefully it made you smile too!'}< /response><Gmap_id>0x80dd35d98069b5c7:0xf59f43d3f0492961</Gmap_id><Date>1494718927906</Date>< username>

Worst Chipotle I ever visited on 8/06/16, and I've been to many throughout LA. Ordered a quesadilla and it barely had any meat. It was beef which costs the most like $8. Might as well have ordered a burrito and could've actually had enough to eat. Cashier told me I had to cut my quesadilla. How the F am I going to cut it myself? A big floppy piece of food cut on top of foil with a plastic knife? The foil will rip.. It goes through and touches the table, that's not sanitary. Maybe that was a new policy that was recent at that time, not sure, but I've never heard that before from any other Chipotle. I normally never ever complain unless it's that bad. Cashier offered me a little cup of beef that I could add myself to my quesadilla. Talked to the manager about everything and of course she tried to buy me off with free coupons. I didn't care about the mishap as much as what was troubling me was all the employees apathetic attitude, no one cared or seemed to desire improvement.
